<script>
function refresh() {
	var species = document.getElementById("speciesbox").value;
	var protocol = document.getElementById("protbox").value;
	var sort = document.getElementById("sortbox").value;

	var url = 'samples.html?species=' + species + '&protocol=' + protocol + '&sort=' + sort;

	window.location.href = url;
}
